3. 识别潜在的性能瓶颈（例如 N+1 查询、频繁内存分配、同步阻塞、热路径锁争用等）

```
<path>/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/index.ts</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: import {
2:     Plugin,
3:     getFrontend,
4: } from "siyuan"
5: 
6: import { svelteDialog } from "./libs/dialog"
7: import { configStore } from "./stores/config"
8: import { destroyBgLayer, createBgLayer, renderImage, renderVideo, changeOpacity, changeBlur, changePosition, setVisible, startAutoRefresh, stopAutoRefresh } from "./services/bgRender"
9: import { scanAll, pickRandom } from "./services/sourceManager"
10: import { diyIcon, pickDefaultBackground, DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS, IMAGE_EXTS, VIDEO_EXTS } from "./constants"
11: import { debug, log } from "./utils/logger"
12: import { isCurrentThemeDisabled, watchTheme } from "./utils/theme"
13: import SettingsPanel from "./ui/settings/settings.svelte"
14: import { buildTopBarMenu } from "./ui/topbar-menu"
15: 
16: export { svelteDialog }
17: 
18: export default class BgCoverPlugin extends Plugin {
19: 
20:     public isMobileLayout: boolean
21:     private _unwatchTheme: (() => void) | null = null
22: 
23:     async onload() {
24:         const frontEnd = getFrontend()
25:         this.isMobileLayout = frontEnd === "mobile" || frontEnd === "browser-mobile"
26: 
27:         await configStore.load()
28: 
29:         await configStore.cleanOldConfigIfNeeded()
30: 
31:         ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin = {
32:             i18n: this.i18n,
33:             isMobileLayout: this.isMobileLayout,
34:             plugin: this,
35:             configStore,
36:         }
37: 
38:         this.addIcons(diyIcon.iconLogo)
39: 
40:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "selectPictureManualLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘F6", callback: () => this.openSetting("sources") })
41:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "selectPictureRandomLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘F7", callback: () => this.randomSelect() })
42:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "openBackgroundLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘F4", callback: () => this.toggleBackground() })
43:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "reduceBackgroundOpacityLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘7", callback: () => {
44:             const v = Math.max(0, configStore.get("opacity") - 0.05)
45:             configStore.setAndSave("opacity", v)
46:             changeOpacity(v)
47:         }})
48:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "addBackgroundOpacityLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘8", callback: () => {
49:             const v = Math.min(1, configStore.get("opacity") + 0.05)
50:             configStore.setAndSave("opacity", v)
51:             changeOpacity(v)
52:         }})
53:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "reduceBackgroundBlurLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘9", callback: () => {
54:             const v = Math.max(0, configStore.get("blur") - 1)
55:             configStore.setAndSave("blur", v)
56:             changeBlur(v)
57:         }})
58:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "addBackgroundBlurLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘0", callback: () => {
59:             const v = Math.min(10, configStore.get("blur") + 1)
60:             configStore.setAndSave("blur", v)
61:             changeBlur(v)
62:         }})
63: 
64:         if (configStore.get("activate")) {
65:             createBgLayer()
66:             if (configStore.get("changeBgOnStart")) {
67:                 await this.randomSelect()
68:             }
69:             const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
70:             if (DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS.includes(currentFile ?? '')) {
71:                 configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
72:                 configStore.save()
73:             }
74:             if (!configStore.get("currentFile")) {
75:                 const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
76:                 const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
77:                 const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)
78:                 if (pool.length === 0) {
79:                     configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
80:                     configStore.save()
81:                 }
82:             }
83:             this.applyBackground()
84:         }
85: 
86:         this._unwatchTheme = watchTheme((mode, name) => {
87:             log("[bgCover] theme changed:", mode, name)
88:             this.applyThemeShield()
89:         })
90: 
91:         log("[bgCover]", this.i18n.helloPlugin)
92:     }
93: 
94:     onLayoutReady() {
95:         const topBarElement = this.addTopBar({
96:             icon: "iconLogo",
97:             title: this.i18n.addTopBarIcon,
98:             position: "right",
99:             callback: () => {
100:                 buildTopBarMenu(topBarElement, this, {
101:                     onOpenSettings: (tab?: string) => this.openSetting(tab),
102:                     toggleBackground: () => this.toggleBackground(),
103:                     randomSelect: () => this.randomSelect(),
104:                 })
105:             },
106:         })
107:     }
108: 
109:     openSetting(activeTab?: string): void {
110:         svelteDialog({
111:             title: "Background Cover",
112:             width: this.isMobileLayout ? "92vw" : "max(520px, 60vw)",
113:             height: "max(520px, 60vh)",
114:             component: SettingsPanel,
115:             props: { activeTab },
116:         })
117:     }
118: 
119:     onunload() {
120:         this._unwatchTheme?.()
121:         destroyBgLayer()
122:         log("[bgCover]", this.i18n.byePlugin)
123:     }
124: 
125:     async toggleBackground() {
126:         const active = !configStore.get("activate")
127:         log("[bgCover] toggleBackground:", active ? "activated" : "deactivated")
128:         configStore.setAndSave("activate", active)
129:         if (active) {
130:             createBgLayer()
131:             this.applyBackground()
132:         } else {
133:             destroyBgLayer()
134:         }
135:     }
136: 
137:     async randomSelect() {
138:         const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
139:         const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
140:         const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)
141:         if (pool.length === 0) {
142:             log("[bgCover] randomSelect: pool is empty, nothing to pick")
143:             return
144:         }
145:         const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get("currentFile") : null
146:         const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)
147:         if (!item) return
148:         log("[bgCover] randomSelect: picked", item.name, "from", pool.length, "items")
149:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
150:         configStore.save()
151:         if (item.type === 'image') {
152:             renderImage(item.url)
153:         } else {
154:             renderVideo(item.url)
155:         }
156:         changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
157:         changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
158:         changePosition(configStore.get("positionX"), configStore.get("positionY"))
159:     }
160: 
161:     private applyBackground() {
162:         log("[bgCover] applyBackground: start")
163:         try {
164:             const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
165:             debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: currentFile =", currentFile)
166:             if (!currentFile) {
167:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: currentFile is null, skip render")
168:                 return
169:             }
170: 
171:             const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
172:             debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: ext =", ext)
173:             if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
174:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderVideo")
175:                 renderVideo(currentFile)
176:             } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
177:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderImage")
178:                 renderImage(currentFile)
179:             } else {
180:                 console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension "${ext}" for ${currentFile}`)
181:                 return
182:             }
183:         } finally {
184:             const opacity = configStore.get("opacity")
185:             const blur = configStore.get("blur")
186:             const px = configStore.get("positionX")
187:             const py = configStore.get("positionY")
188:             debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: changeOpacity =", opacity, "blur =", blur, "pos =", px, py)
189:             changeOpacity(opacity)
190:             changeBlur(blur)
191:             changePosition(px, py)
192:         }
193: 
194:         const interval = configStore.get("autoRefreshTime")
195:         stopAutoRefresh()
196:         if (interval > 0) {
197:             startAutoRefresh(() => this.randomSelect(), interval * 60000)
198:         }
199:     }
200: 
201:     applyThemeShield() {
202:         if (!configStore.get("activate")) return
203:         if (isCurrentThemeDisabled(configStore.get("disabledThemes"))) {
204:             log("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme disabled, hiding")
205:             setVisible(false)
206:         } else {
207:             log("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme enabled, showing")
208:             createBgLayer()
209:             this.applyBackground()
210:         }
211:     }
212: }

(End of file - total 212 lines)
</content>
```

```
44: 
45: export function classifyFileType(filename: string): 'image' | 'video' | null {
46:     const ext = filename.includes('.')
47:         ? '.' + filename.split('.').pop()!.toLowerCase()
48:         : ''
49: 
50:     if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'image'
51:     if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'video'
52:     return null
53: }
```

```
166:             // 内部处理 unmount

168:             if (args.callback) args.callback();
169:         }
170:     });
```

```
1: /*

10: import { Plugin, Setting } from 'siyuan';
11: import { debug } from '../utils/logger';

13: 
14: /**
15:  * The default function to get the value of the element
16:  * @param type 
17:  * @returns 
18:  */
19: const createDefaultGetter = (type: TSettingItemType) => {
20:     let getter: (ele: HTMLElement) => any;
21:     switch (type) {
22:         case 'checkbox':
23:             getter = (ele: HTMLInputElement) => {
24:                 return ele.checked;
25:             };
26:             break;
27:         case 'select':
28:         case 'slider':
29:         case 'textinput':
30:         case 'textarea':
31:             getter = (ele: HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement | HTMLSelectElement) => {
32:                 return ele.value;
33:             };
34:             break;
35:         case 'number':
36:             getter = (ele: HTMLInputElement) => {
37:                 return parseInt(ele.value);
38:             }
39:             break;
40:         default:
41:             getter = () => null;
42:             break;
43:     }
44:     return getter;
45: }
46: 
47: 
48: /**
49:  * The default function to set the value of the element
50:  * @param type 
51:  * @returns 
52:  */
53: const createDefaultSetter = (type: TSettingItemType) => {
54:     let setter: (ele: HTMLElement, value: any) => void;
55:     switch (type) {
56:         case 'checkbox':
57:             setter = (ele: HTMLInputElement, value: any) => {
58:                 ele.checked = value;
59:             };
60:             break;
61:         case 'select':
62:         case 'slider':
63:         case 'textinput':
64:         case 'textarea':
65:         case 'number':
66:             setter = (ele: HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement | HTMLSelectElement, value: any) => {
67:                 ele.value = value;
68:             };
69:             break;
70:         default:
71:             setter = () => {};
72:             break;
73:     }

79: export class SettingUtils {
80:     plugin: Plugin;
81:     name: string;
82:     file: string;
83: 
84:     settings: Map<string, ISettingUtilsItem> = new Map();
85:     elements: Map<string, HTMLElement> = new Map();
86: 
87:     constructor(args: {
88:         plugin: Plugin,
89:         name?: string,
90:         callback?: (data: any) => void,
91:         width?: string,
92:         height?: string
93:     }) {
94:         this.name = args.name ?? 'settings';
95:         this.plugin = args.plugin;
96:         this.file = this.name.endsWith('.json') ? this.name : `${this.name}.json`;
97:         this.plugin.setting = new Setting({
98:             width: args.width,
99:             height: args.height,
100:             confirmCallback: () => {
101:                 for (let key of this.settings.keys()) {
102:                     this.updateValueFromElement(key);
103:                 }
104:                 let data = this.dump();
105:                 if (args.callback !== undefined) {
106:                     args.callback(data);
107:                 }
108:                 this.plugin.data[this.name] = data;
109:                 this.save(data);
110:             },
111:             destroyCallback: () => {
112:                 //Restore the original value
113:                 for (let key of this.settings.keys()) {
114:                     this.updateElementFromValue(key);
115:                 }
116:             }
117:         });
118:     }
119: 
120:     async load() {
121:         let data = await this.plugin.loadData(this.file);
122:         debug('[bgCover] Load config:', data);
123:         if (data) {
124:             for (let [key, item] of this.settings) {
125:                 item.value = data?.[key] ?? item.value;
126:             }
127:         }
128:         this.plugin.data[this.name] = this.dump();
129:         return data;
130:     }
131: 
132:     async save(data?: any) {
133:         data = data ?? this.dump();
134:         await this.plugin.saveData(this.file, this.dump());
135:         debug('[bgCover] Save config:', data);
136:         return data;
137:     }
138: 
139:     /**
140:      * read the data after saving
141:      * @param key key name
142:      * @returns setting item value
143:      */
144:     get(key: string) {
145:         return this.settings.get(key)?.value;
146:     }
147: 
148:     /**
149:      * Set data to this.settings, 
150:      * but do not save it to the configuration file
151:      * @param key key name
152:      * @param value value
153:      */
154:     set(key: string, value: any) {
155:         let item = this.settings.get(key);
156:         if (item) {
157:             item.value = value;
158:             this.updateElementFromValue(key);
159:         }
160:     }
161: 
162:     /**
163:      * Set and save setting item value
164:      * If you want to set and save immediately you can use this method
165:      * @param key key name
166:      * @param value value
167:      */
168:     async setAndSave(key: string, value: any) {
169:         let item = this.settings.get(key);
170:         if (item) {
171:             item.value = value;
172:             this.updateElementFromValue(key);
173:             await this.save();
174:         }
175:     }
176: 
177:     /**
178:       * Read in the value of element instead of setting obj in real time
179:       * @param key key name
180:       * @param apply whether to apply the value to the setting object
181:       *        if true, the value will be applied to the setting object
182:       * @returns value in html
183:       */
184:     take(key: string, apply: boolean = false) {
185:         let item = this.settings.get(key);
186:         let element = this.elements.get(key) as any;
187:         if (!element) {
188:             return
189:         }
190:         if (apply) {
191:             this.updateValueFromElement(key);
192:         }
193:         return item.getEleVal(element);
194:     }
195: 
196:     /**
197:      * Read data from html and save it
198:      * @param key key name
199:      * @param value value
200:      * @return value in html
201:      */
202:     async takeAndSave(key: string) {
203:         let value = this.take(key, true);
204:         await this.save();
205:         return value;
206:     }
207: 
208:     /**
209:      * Disable setting item
210:      * @param key key name
211:      */
212:     disable(key: string) {
213:         let element = this.elements.get(key) as any;
214:         if (element) {
215:             element.disabled = true;
216:         }
217:     }
218: 
219:     /**
220:      * Enable setting item
221:      * @param key key name
222:      */
223:     enable(key: string) {
224:         let element = this.elements.get(key) as any;
225:         if (element) {
226:             element.disabled = false;
227:         }
228:     }
229: 
230:     /**
231:      * 将设置项目导出为 JSON 对象
232:      * @returns object
233:      */
234:     dump(): Object {
235:         let data: any = {};
236:         for (let [key, item] of this.settings) {
237:             if (item.type === 'button') continue;
238:             data[key] = item.value;
239:         }
240:         return data;
241:     }
242: 
243:     addItem(item: ISettingUtilsItem) {
244:         this.settings.set(item.key, item);
245:         const IsCustom = item.type === 'custom';
246:         let error = IsCustom && (item.createElement === undefined || item.getEleVal === undefined || item.setEleVal === undefined);
247:         if (error) {
248:             console.error('The custom setting item must have createElement, getEleVal and setEleVal methods');
249:             return;
250:         }
251: 
252:         if (item.getEleVal === undefined) {
253:             item.getEleVal = createDefaultGetter(item.type);
254:         }
255:         if (item.setEleVal === undefined) {
256:             item.setEleVal = createDefaultSetter(item.type);
257:         }
258: 
259:         if (item.createElement === undefined) {
260:             let itemElement = this.createDefaultElement(item);
261:             this.elements.set(item.key, itemElement);
262:             this.plugin.setting.addItem({
263:                 title: item.title,
264:                 description: item?.description,
265:                 direction: item?.direction,
266:                 createActionElement: () => {
267:                     this.updateElementFromValue(item.key);
268:                     let element = this.getElement(item.key);
269:                     return element;
270:                 }
271:             });
272:         } else {
273:             this.plugin.setting.addItem({
274:                 title: item.title,
275:                 description: item?.description,
276:                 direction: item?.direction,
277:                 createActionElement: () => {
278:                     let val = this.get(item.key);
279:                     let element = item.createElement(val);
280:                     this.elements.set(item.key, element);
281:                     return element;
282:                 }
283:             });
284:         }
285:     }
286: 
287:     createDefaultElement(item: ISettingUtilsItem) {
288:         let itemElement: HTMLElement;
289:         //阻止思源内置的回车键确认
290:         const preventEnterConfirm = (e) => {
291:             if (e.key === 'Enter') {
292:                 e.preventDefault();
293:                 e.stopImmediatePropagation();
294:             }
295:         }
296:         switch (item.type) {
297:             case 'checkbox':
298:                 let element: HTMLInputElement = document.createElement('input');
299:                 element.type = 'checkbox';
300:                 element.checked = item.value;
301:                 element.className = "b3-switch fn__flex-center";
302:                 itemElement = element;
303:                 element.onchange = item.action?.callback ?? (() => { });
304:                 break;
305:             case 'select':
306:                 let selectElement: HTMLSelectElement = document.createElement('select');
307:                 selectElement.className = "b3-select fn__flex-center fn__size200";
308:                 let options = item?.options ?? {};
309:                 for (let val in options) {
310:                     let optionElement = document.createElement('option');
311:                     let text = options[val];
312:                     optionElement.value = val;
313:                     optionElement.text = text;
314:                     selectElement.appendChild(optionElement);
315:                 }
316:                 selectElement.value = item.value;
317:                 selectElement.onchange = item.action?.callback ?? (() => { });
318:                 itemElement = selectElement;
319:                 break;
320:             case 'slider':
321:                 let sliderElement: HTMLInputElement = document.createElement('input');
322:                 sliderElement.type = 'range';
323:                 sliderElement.className = 'b3-slider fn__size200 b3-tooltips b3-tooltips__n';
324:                 sliderElement.ariaLabel = item.value;
325:                 sliderElement.min = item.slider?.min.toString() ?? '0';
326:                 sliderElement.max = item.slider?.max.toString() ?? '100';
327:                 sliderElement.step = item.slider?.step.toString() ?? '1';
328:                 sliderElement.value = item.value;
329:                 sliderElement.onchange = () => {
330:                     sliderElement.ariaLabel = sliderElement.value;
331:                     item.action?.callback();
332:                 }
333:                 itemElement = sliderElement;
334:                 break;
335:             case 'textinput':
336:                 let textInputElement: HTMLInputElement = document.createElement('input');
337:                 textInputElement.className = 'b3-text-field fn__flex-center fn__size200';
338:                 textInputElement.value = item.value;
339:                 textInputElement.onchange = item.action?.callback ?? (() => { });
340:                 itemElement = textInputElement;
341:                 textInputElement.addEventListener('keydown', preventEnterConfirm);
342:                 break;
343:             case 'textarea':
344:                 let textareaElement: HTMLTextAreaElement = document.createElement('textarea');
345:                 textareaElement.className = "b3-text-field fn__block";
346:                 textareaElement.value = item.value;
347:                 textareaElement.onchange = item.action?.callback ?? (() => { });
348:                 itemElement = textareaElement;
349:                 break;
350:             case 'number':
351:                 let numberElement: HTMLInputElement = document.createElement('input');
352:                 numberElement.type = 'number';
353:                 numberElement.className = 'b3-text-field fn__flex-center fn__size200';
354:                 numberElement.value = item.value;
355:                 itemElement = numberElement;
356:                 numberElement.addEventListener('keydown', preventEnterConfirm);
357:                 break;
358:             case 'button':
359:                 let buttonElement: HTMLButtonElement = document.createElement('button');
360:                 buttonElement.className = "b3-button b3-button--outline fn__flex-center fn__size200";
361:                 buttonElement.innerText = item.button?.label ?? 'Button';
362:                 buttonElement.onclick = item.button?.callback ?? (() => { });
363:                 itemElement = buttonElement;
364:                 break;
365:             case 'hint':
366:                 let hintElement: HTMLElement = document.createElement('div');
367:                 hintElement.className = 'b3-label fn__flex-center';
368:                 itemElement = hintElement;
369:                 break;
370:         }
371:         return itemElement;
372:     }
373: 
374:     /**
375:      * return the setting element
376:      * @param key key name
377:      * @returns element
378:      */
379:     getElement(key: string) {
380:         // let item = this.settings.get(key);
381:         let element = this.elements.get(key) as any;
382:         return element;
383:     }
384: 
385:     private updateValueFromElement(key: string) {
386:         let item = this.settings.get(key);
387:         if (item.type === 'button') return;
388:         let element = this.elements.get(key) as any;
389:         item.value = item.getEleVal(element);
390:     }
391: 
392:     private updateElementFromValue(key: string) {
393:         let item = this.settings.get(key);
394:         if (item.type === 'button') return;
395:         let element = this.elements.get(key) as any;
396:         item.setEleVal(element, item.value);
397:     }
398: }

(End of file - total 398 lines)
```

```
25:     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
26:         fetchPost(url, data ?? {}, (response: any) => {
27:             if (response.code === 0) {

35: 
36: class ConfigStore {
37:     private cfg: AppConfig = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
38:     private dirty = false
39:     private ready = false
40: 
41:     async load(): Promise<void> {
42:         if (this.ready) return
43: 
44:         let stored: any = (window as any).siyuan?.storage?.[STORAGE_KEY]
45: 
46:         if (stored === undefined || stored === null) {
47:             try {
48:                 const all = await post<Record<string, any>>("/api/storage/getLocalStorage")
49:                 stored = all?.[STORAGE_KEY] ?? {}
50:             } catch {
51:                 stored = {}
52:             }
53:         }
54: 
55:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS, ...stored }
56:         log("[bgCover] config loaded, keys:", Object.keys(this.cfg))
57:         this.ready = true
58:     }
59: 
60:     async save(): Promise<void> {
61:         if (!this.dirty || !this.ready) return
62:         log("[bgCover] config save")
63:         await post("/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal", {
64:             key: STORAGE_KEY,
65:             val: this.cfg,
66:         })
67:         this.dirty = false
68:     }
69: 
70:     get<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K): AppConfig[K] {
71:         return this.cfg[key]
72:     }
73: 
74:     set<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K, value: AppConfig[K]): void {
75:         this.cfg[key] = value
76:         this.dirty = true
77:     }
78: 
79:     async setAndSave<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K, value: AppConfig[K]): Promise<void> {
80:         this.set(key, value)
81:         await this.save()
82:     }
83: 
84:     snapshot(): Readonly<AppConfig> {
85:         return { ...this.cfg }
86:     }
87: 
88:     async reset(): Promise<void> {
89:         console.log("[bgCover] config reset to defaults")
90:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
91:         this.dirty = true
92:         await this.save()
93: 
94:         try {
95:             await post("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", {
96:                 keys: [STORAGE_KEY],
97:             })
98:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
99: 
100:         try {
101:             await post("/api/file/removeFile", {
102:                 path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/configs.json`,
103:             })
104:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
105: 
106:         await this._cleanPublicDir()
107:     }
108: 
109:     async cleanOldConfigIfNeeded(): Promise<void> {
110:         const stored = (window as any).siyuan?.storage?.[STORAGE_KEY]
111:         if (stored?.crtBgObj !== undefined || stored?.bgObjCfg !== undefined) {
112:             console.log("[bgCover] 检测到旧版配置 (siyuan.storage)，自动重置为默认")
113:             await post("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", { keys: [STORAGE_KEY] })
114:             this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
115:             return
116:         }
117: 
118:         try {
119:             const files = await post<any[]>("/api/file/readDir", {
120:                 path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/`
121:             })
122:             if (Array.isArray(files) && files.length > 0) {
123:                 console.log("[bgCover] 检测到旧版 petal 数据，自动清理")
124:                 await post("/api/file/removeFile", { path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/` })
125:             }
126:         } catch {
127:             debug("[bgCover] cleanOldConfigIfNeeded: petal dir not found")
128:         }
129:     }
130: 
131:     private async _cleanPublicDir(): Promise<void> {
132:         try {
133:             const files = await post<any[]>("/api/file/readDir", {
134:                 path: `/data/public/${STORAGE_KEY}/`,
135:             })
136:             if (!Array.isArray(files)) return
137:             for (const file of files) {
138:                 if (file.isDir) continue
139:                 try {
140:                     await post("/api/file/removeFile", {
141:                         path: `/data/public/${STORAGE_KEY}/${file.name}`,
142:                     })
143:                 } catch { /* ignore */ }
144:             }
145:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
146:     }
147: 
148:     _resetForTest(): void {
149:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
150:         this.dirty = false
151:         this.ready = false
152:     }
153: }
154: 
155: export const configStore = new ConfigStore()

(End of file - total 155 lines)
</content>
```

```
12:     name: string
13: }
14: 
15: async function request(url: string, data: any): Promise<any> {
16:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost(url, data)
17:     return res.code === 0 ? res.data : null
18: }
19: 
20: export async function readDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {
21:     const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
22:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
23:     return (data as IDirItem[])
24:         .filter(item => !item.isDir)
25:         .map(item => item.name)
26: }
27: 
28: export async function fileExistsRemote(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
29:     if (!path) return false
30:     const parentPath = path.substring(0, path.lastIndexOf('/'))
31:     const targetName = path.substring(path.lastIndexOf('/') + 1)
32:     const files = await readDir(parentPath)
33:     return files.includes(targetName)
34: }
35: 
36: export async function readDirItems(path: string): Promise<IDirItem[]> {
37:     const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
38:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
39:     return data as IDirItem[]
40: }
41: 
42: export async function putFile(path: string, file: File | Blob): Promise<boolean> {
43:     const formData = new FormData()
44:     formData.append("path", path)
45:     formData.append("isDir", "false")
46:     formData.append("modTime", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())
47:     formData.append("file", file)
48: 
49:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/putFile", formData)
50:     return res.code === 0
51: }
52: 
53: export async function removeFile(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
54:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/removeFile", { path })
55:     return res.code === 0
56: }
57: 
58: export async function downloadUrl(url: string, destPath: string): Promise<boolean> {
59:     try {
60:         const response = await fetch(url)
61:         if (!response.ok) return false
62:         const blob = await response.blob()
63:         return await putFile(destPath, blob)
64:     } catch (err: any) {
65:         debug('[bgCover] api.ts downloadUrl 失败:', url, err.message)
66:         return false
67:     }
68: }
```

```
35: export function getFileUrl(apiPath: string, sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'): string {
36:     if (sourceType === 'local') {
37:         return `file://${apiPath.replace(/\\/g, '/')}`
38:     }
39: 
40:     let rel = apiPath
41:     if (rel.startsWith('/data/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
42:     if (rel.startsWith('data/')) rel = rel.slice(5)
43:     else if (rel.startsWith('/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
44:     return rel
45: }
```

```
70:     })
```

```
16:

18:     results.push(...uploadItems)
19:     debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll upload: ${uploadItems.length} 个文件`)

34:             if (!ok) {

40:             debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local[${dir}]: ${items.length} 个文件`)

52:     path: string,
53: ): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
54:     const filenames = type === 'local'
55:         ? await readLocalDir(path)
56:         : await readDirKernel(path)

66:             continue

74:             name,
75:             url,
76:             apiPath,
77:             type: fileType,
78:             sourceType: type,
79:             sourceLabel: getSourceLabel(type, path),
80:         })
81:     }
82: 
83:     if (skipped.length > 0) {
84:         debug(`${ENGINE} scanSource[${type}] 跳过不可识别的文件: [${skipped.join(', ')}]`)
85:     }
86: 
87:     return items
88: }

90: export function pickRandom(items: ImageItem[], excludeUrl?: string | null): ImageItem | null {
91:     if (items.length === 0) return null
92: 
93:     if (excludeUrl) {
94:         const filtered = items.filter(item => item.url !== excludeUrl)
95:         if (filtered.length === 0) return null
96:         const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * filtered.length)
97:         return filtered[idx]
98:     }
99: 
100:     const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * items.length)
101:     return items[idx]
102: }
103:

107:     if (isDesktop()) {
108:         try {
109:             await (window as any).require('fs/promises').access(path)
110:             return true
111:         } catch {
112:             return false
113:         }
114:     }
115: 
116:     try {
117:         await readDirKernel(path)
118:         return true
119:     } catch {
120:         return false
121:     }
122: }
123: 
124: function getSourceLabel(type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets', path: string): string {
125:     switch (type) {
126:         case 'upload':
127:             return 'upload'
128:         case 'assets':
129:             return toAssetRelPath(path)
130:         case 'local':
131:             return path
132:     }
133: }
```

```
14:     const clean = url.split('?')[0]
15:     const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
16:     if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'video'
17:     if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) return 'image'
18:     return null
19: }
20: 
21: export function createBgLayer(): void {
22:     if (canvasEl || videoEl) return
23: 
24:     canvasEl = document.createElement('canvas')
25:     canvasEl.id = 'bglayer'
26:     canvasEl.style.backgroundRepeat = 'no-repeat'
27:     canvasEl.style.backgroundAttachment = 'fixed'
28:     canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
29:     canvasEl.style.backgroundPosition = '50% 50%'
30:     canvasEl.style.width = '100%'

33:     canvasEl.style.zIndex = '-10000'

35:

37:     videoEl.id = 'bgvideo'
38:     videoEl.autoplay = true
39:     videoEl.loop = true
40:     videoEl.muted = true

52:     htmlEl.insertBefore(canvasEl, document.head)
53:     htmlEl.insertBefore(videoEl, document.head)
54: }

68:     if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)
69:     else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)
70: }
71: 
72: export function renderImage(url: string): void {
73:     if (!canvasEl) return
74:     log("[bgCover] renderImage:", url.split('/').pop())
75:     currentMode = 'image'
76: 
77:     if (videoEl) {
78:         videoEl.style.display = 'none'
79:         try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
80:         videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
81:     }
82:     canvasEl.style.display = ''
83:     canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
84: }
85: 
86: export function renderVideo(url: string): void {
87:     if (!videoEl) return
88:     log("[bgCover] renderVideo:", url.split('/').pop())
89:     currentMode = 'video'
90: 
91:     if (canvasEl) canvasEl.style.display = 'none'
92:     videoEl.style.display = ''
93:     videoEl.src = url
94:     const playPromise = videoEl.play()
95:     if (playPromise) {
96:         playPromise.catch((e) => {
97:             if (e.name !== 'AbortError') {
98:                 console.warn('[bgCover] video play failed:', e)
99:             }
100:         })
101:     }
102: }
103: 
104: export function clearLayer(): void {
105:     log("[bgCover] clearLayer")
106:     if (canvasEl) {
107:         canvasEl.style.display = 'none'
108:         canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = ''
109:     }
110:     if (videoEl) {
111:         videoEl.style.display = 'none'
112:         try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* not implemented in jsdom */ }
113:         videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
114:     }
115:     currentMode = null
116: }
117: 
118: export function setVisible(visible: boolean): void {
119:     log("[bgCover] setVisible:", visible)
120:     if (canvasEl) canvasEl.style.display = visible && currentMode === 'image' ? '' : 'none'
121:     if (videoEl) videoEl.style.display = visible && currentMode === 'video' ? '' : 'none'
122:     if (!visible) {
123:         document.body.style.removeProperty('opacity')
124:     }
125: }
126: 
127: export function changeOpacity(raw: number): void {
128:     const clamped = Math.max(0.1, Math.min(1, raw))
129:     const opacity = 0.99 - 0.25 * clamped
130:     document.body.style.opacity = String(opacity)
131: }
132: 
133: export function changeBlur(val: number): void {
134:     const px = Math.max(0, Math.min(10, val))
135:     const filter = px > 0 ? `blur(${px}px)` : ''
136: 
137:     if (currentMode === 'image' && canvasEl) {
138:         canvasEl.style.filter = filter
139:     } else if (currentMode === 'video' && videoEl) {
140:         videoEl.style.filter = filter
141:     }
142: }
143: 
144: export function changePosition(x: number, y: number): void {
145:     if (currentMode === 'image' && canvasEl) {
146:         canvasEl.style.backgroundPosition = `${x}% ${y}%`
147:     } else if (currentMode === 'video' && videoEl) {
148:         videoEl.style.objectPosition = `${x}% ${y}%`
149:     }
150: }
151: 
152: export function applyOverrides(x?: number, y?: number, defaultX?: number, defaultY?: number): void {
153:     const posX = x ?? defaultX ?? 50
154:     const posY = y ?? defaultY ?? 50
155:     changePosition(posX, posY)
156: }
157: 
158: export function startAutoRefresh(callback: () => void, intervalMs: number): void {
159:     stopAutoRefresh()
160:     if (intervalMs <= 0) return
161:     log("[bgCover] startAutoRefresh: interval =", intervalMs, "ms")
162:     autoRefreshTimer = setInterval(callback, intervalMs)
163: }
164: 
165: export function stopAutoRefresh(): void {
166:     if (autoRefreshTimer !== null) {
167:         log("[bgCover] stopAutoRefresh")
168:         clearInterval(autoRefreshTimer)
169:         autoRefreshTimer = null
170:     }
171: }

(End of file - total 171 lines)
</content>
```

```
9:     let disabledThemes = $state(configStore.get("disabledThemes"))
10:     let lightItems = $state<ThemeInfo[]>([])
11:     let darkItems = $state<ThemeInfo[]>([])
12:     let currentMode = $state(0)
13:     let currentThemeName = $state('')
14: 
15:     onMount(() => {
16:         const [light, dark] = getInstalledThemes()
17:         lightItems = light
18:         darkItems = dark
19:         const [mode, name] = getCurrentThemeInfo()
20:         currentMode = mode
21:         currentThemeName = name
22:     })
23: 
24:     $effect(() => {
25:         disabledThemes = configStore.get("disabledThemes")
26:     })
27: 
28:     function toggleTheme(mode: 'light' | 'dark', name: string) {
29:         const dt = configStore.get("disabledThemes")
30:         const key = mode === 'light' ? 'light' : 'dark'
31:         const list = [...dt[key]]
32:         const idx = list.indexOf(name)
33:         if (idx >= 0) list.splice(idx, 1)
34:         else list.push(name)
35:         configStore.setAndSave("disabledThemes", { ...dt, [key]: list })
36:         ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.applyThemeShield?.()
37:     }
38: </script>
39: 
40: <div class="config__tab-container" data-name="theme">
41:     <div class="config-bazaar__panel">
42: 
43:         <div class="fn__flex config-bazaar__title">
44:             <div>{i18n.lightThemes}</div>
45:         </div>
46:         <div class="config-bazaar__content">
47:             {#if lightItems.length === 0}
48:                 <div style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface); padding: 8px;">
49:                     {i18n.noLightThemes}
50:                 </div>
51:             {:else}
52:                 <div class="b3-cards">
53:                     {#each lightItems as theme (theme.name)}
54:                         <div class="b3-card b3-card--wrap">
55:                             <div class="fn__flex-1 fn__flex-column">
56:                                 <div class="b3-card__info b3-card__info--left fn__flex-1">
57:                                     <span
58:                                         style:color={currentMode === 0 && currentThemeName === theme.name
59:                                             ? 'var(--b3-theme-primary)' : ''}
60:                                     >
61:                                         {theme.name}
62:                                         {#if currentMode === 0 && currentThemeName === theme.name}
63:                                             {i18n.currentThemeLabel}
64:                                         {/if}
65:                                     </span>
66:                                     <div class="b3-card__desc">{theme.label}</div>
67:                                 </div>
68:                             </div>
69:                             <div class="b3-card__actions b3-card__actions--right">
70:                                 <span class="fn__space"></span>
71:                                 <input class="b3-switch fn__flex-center" type="checkbox"
72:                                     checked={disabledThemes.light.includes(theme.name)}
73:                                     onchange={() => toggleTheme('light', theme.name)}
74:                                 />
75:                             </div>
76:                         </div>
77:                     {/each}
78:                 </div>
79:             {/if}
80:         </div>
81: 
82:         <div class="fn__flex config-bazaar__title">
83:             <div>{i18n.darkThemes}</div>
84:         </div>
85:         <div class="config-bazaar__content">
86:             {#if darkItems.length === 0}
87:                 <div style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface); padding: 8px;">
88:                     {i18n.noDarkThemes}
89:                 </div>
90:             {:else}
91:                 <div class="b3-cards">
92:                     {#each darkItems as theme (theme.name)}
93:                         <div class="b3-card b3-card--wrap">
94:                             <div class="fn__flex-1 fn__flex-column">
95:                                 <div class="b3-card__info b3-card__info--left fn__flex-1">
96:                                     <span
97:                                         style:color={currentMode === 1 && currentThemeName === theme.name
98:                                             ? 'var(--b3-theme-primary)' : ''}
99:                                     >
100:                                         {theme.name}
101:                                         {#if currentMode === 1 && currentThemeName === theme.name}
102:                                             {i18n.currentThemeLabel}
103:                                         {/if}
104:                                     </span>
105:                                     <div class="b3-card__desc">{theme.label}</div>
106:                                 </div>
107:                             </div>
108:                             <div class="b3-card__actions b3-card__actions--right">
109:                                 <span class="fn__space"></span>
110:                                 <input class="b3-switch fn__flex-center" type="checkbox"
111:                                     checked={disabledThemes.dark.includes(theme.name)}
112:                                     onchange={() => toggleTheme('dark', theme.name)}
113:                                 />
114:                             </div>
115:                         </div>
116:                     {/each}
117:                 </div>

119:         </div>
```

```
<content>
1: <script lang="ts">
2:     import { onMount } from "svelte"
3:     import { readDirItems } from "../../utils/api"
4:     import { classifyFileType } from "../../types"
5:     import { configStore } from "../../stores/config"
6:     import { toAssetRelPath } from "../../utils/path"
7:     import { log } from "../../utils/logger"
8: 
9:     const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}
10: 
11:     interface DirNode {
12:         name: string
13:         path: string
14:         imageCount: number
15:         videoCount: number
16:         children: DirNode[]
17:         open: boolean
18:         loaded: boolean
19:         hasSubdirs: boolean
20:     }
21: 
22:     interface Props {
23:         onConfirm?: (selectedPaths: string[]) => void
24:     }
25: 
26:     let { onConfirm }: Props = $props()
27: 
28:     let roots = $state<DirNode[]>([])
29:     let selectedDir = $state<string | null>(null)
30:     let loading = $state(true)
31: 
32:     async function scanDir(dirPath: string): Promise<{
33:         imageCount: number; videoCount: number; hasSubdirs: boolean; childDirs: string[]
34:     }> {
35:         let imageCount = 0, videoCount = 0, hasSubdirs = false
36:         const childDirs: string[] = []
37:         const items = await readDirItems(dirPath + '/')
38:         for (const child of items) {
39:             if (child.isDir) {
40:                 hasSubdirs = true
41:                 childDirs.push(child.name)
42:             } else {
43:                 const type = classifyFileType(child.name)
44:                 if (type === 'image') imageCount++
45:                 else if (type === 'video') videoCount++
46:             }
47:         }
48:         return { imageCount, videoCount, hasSubdirs, childDirs }
49:     }
50: 
51:     onMount(async () => {
52:         const items = await readDirItems("/data/assets/")
53:         for (const item of items) {
54:             if (!item.isDir) continue
55:             const nodePath = "/data/assets/" + item.name
56:             const { imageCount, videoCount, hasSubdirs } = await scanDir(nodePath)
57:             roots.push({
58:                 name: item.name,
59:                 path: nodePath,
60:                 imageCount,
61:                 videoCount,
62:                 children: [],
63:                 open: false,
64:                 loaded: false,
65:                 hasSubdirs,
66:             })
67:         }
68:         roots.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name))
69:         loading = false
70:     })
71: 
72:     async function expandChild(node: DirNode) {
73:         if (node.open) {
74:             node.open = false
75:             return
76:         }
77: 
78:         if (!node.loaded) {
79:             log("[bgCover] assetPicker expand:", node.name)
80:             node.imageCount = 0
81:             node.videoCount = 0
82:             node.children = []
83: 
84:             const items = await readDirItems(node.path + '/')
85:             for (const child of items) {
86:                 if (child.isDir) {
87:                     const childPath = node.path + '/' + child.name
88:                     const { imageCount, videoCount, hasSubdirs } = await scanDir(childPath)
89:                     node.children.push({
90:                         name: child.name,
91:                         path: childPath,
92:                         imageCount,
93:                         videoCount,
94:                         children: [],
95:                         open: false,
96:                         loaded: false,
97:                         hasSubdirs,
98:                     })
99:                 } else {
100:                     const type = classifyFileType(child.name)
101:                     if (type === 'image') node.imageCount++
102:                     else if (type === 'video') node.videoCount++
103:                 }
104:             }
105:             node.children.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name))
106:             node.loaded = true
107:         }
108: 
109:         node.open = true
110:     }
111: 
112:     function selectDir(path: string, total: number) {
113:         if (total > 0) selectedDir = path
114:     }
115: 
116:     function getRelPath(fullPath: string): string {
117:         return toAssetRelPath(fullPath)
118:     }
119: 
120:     function confirm() {
121:         if (!selectedDir) return
122:         const rel = getRelPath(selectedDir)
123:         log("[bgCover] assetPicker confirm:", rel)
124:         onConfirm?.([rel])
125:     }
126: 
127:     function isAlreadyAdded(nodePath: string): boolean {
128:         return configStore.get("assetDirs").includes(getRelPath(nodePath))
129:     }
130: </script>
131: 
132: <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 8px; padding: 8px; width: 100%;">
133:     <div class="b3-list b3-list--border b3-list--background" style="max-height: 400px; overflow-y: auto;">
134:         {#if loading}
135:             <div class="b3-list-item" style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface); padding: 16px; text-align: center;">
136:                 {i18n.loading}
137:             </div>
138:         {:else if roots.length === 0}
139:             <div class="b3-list-item" style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface); padding: 16px; text-align: center;">
140:                 {i18n.noFolderSelected}
141:             </div>
142:         {:else}
143:             {#each roots as root (root.path)}
144:                 {@const rTotal = root.imageCount + root.videoCount}
145:                 <div
146:                     class="b3-list-item b3-list-item--narrow toggle"
147:                     class:b3-list-item--focus={selectedDir === root.path}
148:                     style:opacity={rTotal > 0 ? "1" : "0.45"}
149:                     onclick={() => selectDir(root.path, rTotal)}
150:                     onkeydown={undefined}
151:                     role="button"
152:                     tabindex="0"
153:                 >
154:                     {#if root.hasSubdirs}
155:                         <span class="b3-list-item__toggle b3-list-item__toggle--hl"
156:                             onclick={(e: MouseEvent) => { e.stopPropagation(); expandChild(root) }}
157:                             onkeydown={undefined}
158:                             role="button"
159:                             tabindex="0">
160:                             <svg class="b3-list-item__arrow" class:b3-list-item__arrow--open={root.open}>
161:                                 <use xlink:href="#iconRight"></use>
162:                             </svg>
163:                         </span>
164:                     {/if}
165:                     <span class="b3-list-item__text fn__flex-1"
166:                         style:color={isAlreadyAdded(root.path) ? 'var(--b3-theme-primary)' : ''}>
167:                         <svg style="width:14px;height:14px;margin-right:4px;vertical-align:middle">
168:                             <use xlink:href="#iconFolder"></use>
169:                         </svg>
170:                         {root.name}/
171:                         <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface); font-size: 0.85em; margin-left: 8px;">
172:                             ({rTotal} {i18n.imageCount}, {root.videoCount} {i18n.videoCount})
173:                         </span>
174:                     </span>
175:                     {#if isAlreadyAdded(root.path)}
176:                         <span class="b3-list-item__action" style="color: var(--b3-theme-primary)">

178:                         </span>
179:                     {/if}
180:                 </div>
181: 
182:                 {#if root.open}
183:                     <div class="b3-list__panel">
184:                         {#each root.children as child (child.path)}
185:                             {@const cTotal = child.imageCount + child.videoCount}
186:                             <div
187:                                 class="b3-list-item b3-list-item--narrow toggle"
188:                                 class:b3-list-item--focus={selectedDir === child.path}
189:                                 style:opacity={cTotal > 0 ? "1" : "0.45"}
190:                                 onclick={() => selectDir(child.path, cTotal)}
191:                                 onkeydown={undefined}
```

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now I have read all the source files. Let me conduct a thorough code quality review based on the user's three areas:

1. Module division, dependency direction, coupling, single responsibility, over-design/tech debt
2. Architecture clarity, naming consistency, function/variable length, comments
3. Performance bottlenecks

Let me analyze each area systematically.

## 1. Module Division & Architecture

### Architecture Diagram (Dependency Direction):
```
index.ts (plugin entry)
├── libs/ (framework-level)
│   ├── dialog.ts - uses "siyuan" Dialog
│   ├── setting-utils.ts - uses "siyuan" Plugin/Setting
│   └── index.d.ts - type declarations
├── services/ (core business logic)
│   ├── bgRender.ts - canvas/video manipulation (no siyuan imports except constants)
│   └── sourceManager.ts - scans sources (uses utils/fs, utils/api)
├── stores/
│   └── config.ts - config state management (uses "siyuan" fetchPost)
├── utils/ (business utilities)
│   ├── api.ts - kernel API wrapper (uses fetchSyncPost)
│   ├── fs.ts - local filesystem (uses stores/config)
│   ├── logger.ts - logging (uses stores/config)
│   ├── path.ts - path utilities
│   └── theme.ts - theme detection
├── ui/
│   ├── topbar-menu.ts - topbar menu builder
│   ├── settings/ - settings panel tabs
│   ├── sources/ - source list & asset picker
│   ├── local-dir-dialog.svelte
│   └── url-dialog.svelte
├── types.ts - type definitions & classifyFileType
├── constants.ts - constants
└── types/index.d.ts - siyuan type declarations
```

### Module Analysis:

**Good aspects:**
1. Clear separation: libs (framework), services (core logic), stores (state), utils (tools), ui (views)
2. The dependency direction is mostly correct: ui → services/stores/utils, services → utils/stores
3. `types.ts` is concise and well-organized
4. `constants.ts` is well-structured

**Issues found:**

**I1. `utils/fs.ts` depends on `stores/config.ts` - violates the dependency rule**
The fs module should be a pure utility, but it imports configStore to implement `isLocalPath()`. This creates a circular-like dependency where a low-level utility depends on the store layer. The `isLocalPath` function is about config data, not filesystem operations.

**I2. `classifyFileType` is placed in `types.ts`** - it's a function, not a type. It should be in utils or constants. This makes types.ts a mixed bag of types and logic.

**I3. Duplicate code in `topbar-menu.ts` and `sources-tab.svelte`** - Both files have identical implementations of `pickMultipleFiles()`, `pickFolderFiles()`, `showUrlDialog()`, `showAssetsDirDialog()`, and `showLocalDirDialog()`. This is a DRY violation likely caused by the menu being extracted from the original settings panel as a separate entry point but without sharing the implementations.

**I4. `handleActivateChange` in `config-tab.svelte` only calls `renderImage()`** even when `currentFile` could be a video. This is a bug (missing `render` dispatch).

**I5. `bgRender.ts` uses module-level mutable state** (canvasEl, videoEl, currentMode, autoRefreshTimer). This works for a single-instance plugin but makes testing harder and prevents any future multi-window support. Consider encapsulating in a class.

**I6. `configStore` is a singleton exported at module level** - This means it's hard to test in isolation, though the `_resetForTest()` method exists as a workaround.

**I7. `src/index.ts` at 212 lines** - Exceeds the 50-line-per-function rule but given it's the plugin entry point wiring everything together, this is acceptable. However, the `onload()` method at ~70 lines could be decomposed.

**I8. Missing abstraction for file upload** - The upload logic (FormData construction, path calculation) is repeated in `topbar-menu.ts` (lines 65-69) and `utils/api.ts` (putFile). In topbar-menu, pickMultipleFiles uses raw fetchPost instead of the `putFile` wrapper from api.ts, while pickFolderFiles does use apiPutFile. This inconsistency is tech debt.

**I9. `validatePath` in sourceManager.ts** - Has duplicated logic with `fs.ts` (access check), using inline `require('fs/promises')` instead of the existing `readLocalDir` / `getFsp` abstractions. 

## 2. Naming & Clarity

**Good:**
- Most function names are descriptive and follow camelCase convention
- Svelte component names follow PascalCase
- Constants use UPPER_SNAKE_CASE

**Issues:**

**N1. `post` function in `stores/config.ts`** - Too generic. It wraps fetchPost but the name doesn't indicate it's an API call. Suggest: `apiPost` or `kernelPost`.

**N2. `readDir` in `utils/api.ts` vs `readLocalDir` in `utils/fs.ts`** - The api version is imported as `readDirKernel` in sourceManager.ts but its real name is `readDir`. This aliasing creates confusion. Suggest renaming: `readRemoteDir` / `readLocalDir`, or consistently use `readKernelDir`.

**N3. `scanAll` and `scanSource` in sourceManager** - `scanSource` suggests it scans one source, but it accepts a path parameter for any type. The naming is actually fine when seen together.

**N4. `log` and `debug` functions in logger.ts** - Overly generic names that conflict with global `console.log`/`console.debug`. But they're imported explicitly so it's acceptable. However, both functions only log when `inDev` is true - `log` could be renamed to `devLog` to be clearer.

**N5. `bgRender.ts` exports flat functions** - Functions like `changeOpacity`, `changeBlur`, `changePosition` are clear but the module-level state makes it look like a procedural script rather than a service.

**N6. `ENGINE` constant in sourceManager.ts** - Used once, only for debug prefix. Could just inline `'[bgCover] sourceManager'`.

**N7. `VALID_EXTS` in url-dialog.svelte** - Redefined locally instead of importing IMAGE_EXTS and VIDEO_EXTS from constants. This duplicates the list and could drift.

**N8. In `index.ts` line 91**, the log message `helloPlugin` i18n key name is not self-documenting - "helloPlugin" is a generic greeting key. Fine if the i18n JSON has meaningful content.

**N9. `diyIcon` in constants.ts** - "diy" is a typo for "diy" (should be a Chinese-English mix meaning "custom"). Suggest: `pluginIcon` or `customIcon`.

**N10. The `buildAddBackgroundSubmenu` in topbar-menu.ts returns `any[]`** - Should have a proper type definition.

**N11. `_cleanPublicDir` method** - Private method uses underscore prefix (Python convention). In TypeScript, `private` keyword is sufficient.

**N12. Comments**: Most files have no function-level comments (except setting-utils.ts which has some docstrings). The code is fairly self-documenting for an experienced developer, but for a plugin that may have community contributors, more JSDoc would help.

## 3. Performance Bottlenecks

**P1. `scanAll` in `sourceManager.ts` - Sequential directory scanning**
Each asset directory and local folder is scanned sequentially with `for...of` loops and `await`. For users with many folders, this means N sequential network/filesystem calls. The total time = sum of all scan times.
**Suggestion**: Use `Promise.all` to parallelize independent scans.

**P2. `scanSource` creates intermediate arrays**
For each file, it creates an ImageItem object. With thousands of files, this allocates many objects. The `spread` operator in `results.push(...uploadItems)` also creates intermediate arrays.
**Impact**: Minor for typical use (10-1000 files). Only problematic at scale.

**P3. `asset-picker.svelte` - Sequential directory enumeration**
`onMount` scans root dirs sequentially, and `scanDir` reads each child sequentially.
**Suggestion**: Parallelize with `Promise.all`.

**P4. `topbar-menu.ts` pickMultipleFiles - Sequential uploads**
Each file is uploaded sequentially in a `for` loop with `await`. For N files, this is N sequential HTTP requests.
**Suggestion**: Use `Promise.all` with a concurrency limit (e.g., 5 concurrent uploads).

**P5. `sources-tab.svelte` `refreshAll` - Sequential group scanning**
Each group in assetDirs and localFolders is scanned sequentially. Same issue as scanAll.

**P6. `loadPreview` in sources-tab.svelte**
Every mouse hover on a file triggers `fetch(url) → blob()` to create a preview. This:
- Creates a full HTTP request per hover
- Creates an ObjectURL via `createObjectURL` (and properly revokes with URL.revokeObjectURL)
This is correct behavior but could be optimized with a simple debounce to avoid rapid-fire fetches during fast mouse movement.

**P7. `configStore.save()` - dbounce-like with dirty flag**
The `dirty` flag prevents unnecessary saves, which is good. However, `setAndSave` always saves immediately. Multiple rapid calls to `setAndSave` (e.g., slider dragging on opacity) will cause many API calls. The config-tab.svelte handles this by using `oninput` for visual feedback and `onchange` for persistence - good design.

**P8. `pickRandom` in sourceManager - array filtering and copy**
For the exclude case, `items.filter()` creates a new array copy. With thousands of items, this is O(n) memory allocation.
**Suggestion**: Use random index with retry loop instead of filtering:
```
function pickRandom(items, excludeUrl?) {
    if (items.length === 0) return null
    if (!excludeUrl || items.length === 1) return items[Math.floor(Math.random() * items.length)]
    // Retry up to 10 times
    for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        const item = items[Math.floor(Math.random() * items.length)]
        if (item.url !== excludeUrl) return item
    }
    // Fallback: filter
    const filtered = items.filter(item => item.url !== excludeUrl)
    return filtered.length ? filtered[Math.floor(Math.random() * filtered.length)] : null
}
```

**P9. `MutationObserver` in theme.ts watches `data-theme-mode` on document.documentElement**
This is correct and efficient - it only triggers on attribute changes.

**P10. No hot-path issues or lock contention** - Single-threaded JavaScript in a plugin context means no true concurrency issues.

### Summary of Critical Issues (ordered by severity):

1. **DRY Violation**: Duplicate upload/dialog logic between `topbar-menu.ts` and `sources-tab.svelte` - should be extracted into shared helper functions
2. **Bug**: `config-tab.svelte:handleActivateChange` only calls `renderImage()`, ignoring video files
3. **Dependency Inversion**: `utils/fs.ts` imports `stores/config.ts` (low-level → high-level)
4. **Inconsistent API usage**: `topbar-menu.ts` pickMultipleFiles uses raw `fetchPost` instead of `apiPutFile`
5. **Sequential I/O**: All directory scans and multi-file uploads are sequential instead of parallel
6. **`classifyFileType` location**: Function in a types file
7. **Missing type definition**: `buildAddBackgroundSubmenu` returns `any[]`
8. **`VALID_EXTS` duplication**: Redefined in url-dialog instead of using constants

Let me present this as a comprehensive review.

</details>

下面是对 `src/` 的完整代码审查。

---

## 1. 模块划分、依赖方向与耦合度

### 依赖关系图

```
index.ts (入口点)
├── libs/ (框架层 - 无业务依赖)
│   ├── dialog.ts        → svelte + siyuan Dialog
│   └── setting-utils.ts → siyuan Plugin/Setting
├── services/ (核心业务)
│   ├── bgRender.ts      → constants
│   └── sourceManager.ts → utils/{fs,api,path,logger}, constants
├── stores/
│   └── config.ts        → siyuan fetchPost
├── utils/ (业务工具)
│   ├── api.ts           → siyuan fetchSyncPost
│   ├── fs.ts            → ⚠️ stores/config
│   ├── logger.ts        → ⚠️ stores/config
│   ├── path.ts          → 无外部依赖
│   └── theme.ts         → logger
├── ui/                  → siyuan, services, stores, utils, libs
└── types.ts             → constants (共享)
```

### 发现

| # | 严重度 | 问题 |
|---|--------|------|
| I1 | ⚠️ 中 | **`utils/fs.ts` 导入 `stores/config.ts`** — 底层工具不应该依赖状态层。`isLocalPath()` 是配置查询而非文件系统操作。应移到 `stores/config.ts` 或独立的路径工具函数中。 |
| I2 | ⚠️ 中 | **`classifyFileType` 放在 `types.ts`** — `types.ts` 应该纯定义类型，不应包含业务逻辑函数。建议移到 `utils/fileType.ts` 或合并到 `constants.ts`。 |
| I3 | 🔴 高 | **重复代码** — `topbar-menu.ts` 和 `sources-tab.svelte` 中都有 `pickMultipleFiles`、`pickFolderFiles`、`showAssetsDirDialog`、`showLocalDirDialog`、`showUrlDialog` 的几乎完全相同的实现。应提取到 `ui/upload-actions.ts` 等共享模块。 |
| I4 | 🔴 高 | **Bug：`config-tab.svelte:handleActivateChange`** 只调用 `renderImage()`，即使 `currentFile` 是视频。应改为使用 `render(file.url)` 或其他分派方式。 |
| I5 | ⚠️ 中 | **不一致的 API 使用** — `topbar-menu.ts` 的 `pickMultipleFiles` 用原始 `fetchPost` 构造 FormData，而 `pickFolderFiles` 用 `apiPutFile`。前者绕过 `api.ts` 封装层。 |
| I6 | 💡 低 | **`bgRender.ts` 模块级可变状态** — `canvasEl`、`videoEl`、`currentMode` 是全局变量。对单例插件没问题，但用类封装后会更容易测试，也便于未来扩展。 |
| I7 | 💡 低 | **`validatePath` 在 `sourceManager.ts` 中** — 内联调用 `require('fs/promises')`，而非复用 `fs.ts` 中的 `getFsp`/`fileExistsLocal` 抽象。 |
| I8 | 💡 低 | **`configStore` 是模块级单例** — 工作正常但不够灵活。`_resetForTest()` 变通方法证实了这一点。对于真正的单例模式，可考虑 `instanceof` 守卫以防意外多次实例化。 |

---

## 2. 命名与清晰度

### 良好实践
- 函数命名总体使用驼峰式，且具有描述性
- Svelte 组件使用 PascalCase
- 遵守规则：`libs/` vs `utils/` vs `services/` 职责清晰

### 需要改进的命名

| # | 位置 | 当前名称 | 建议 | 理由 |
|---|------|---------|-----------|--------|
| N1 | `stores/config.ts:24` | `post()` | `kernelPost()` 或 `apiPost()` | 过于泛化，与 HTTP POST 以外的东西冲突 |
| N2 | `utils/api.ts:20` | `readDir()` | `readRemoteDir()` | 与 `utils/fs.ts` 中的 `readLocalDir` 形成对称，避免在 `sourceManager.ts:2` 中需要别名 `readDirKernel` |
| N3 | `utils/logger.ts:11` | `log()` | `devLog()` | "log" 过于泛化；实际行为仅在开发模式下输出，应该用名字体现 |
| N4 | `constants.ts:26` | `diyIcon` | `pluginIcon` 或 `customIcon` | 避免非标准缩写（"diy" 是 "DIY/custom" 的变体形式） |
| N5 | `sourceManager.ts:9` | `ENGINE` | 内联使用 | 作为类外模块级常量仅使用一次作为调试前缀，应内联或改用 `LOG_PREFIX` |
| N6 | `sources-tab.svelte:32-33` | `prevUrl` | `previewObjectUrl` | “prev”容易和“previous”混淆；它实际上是一个 `createObjectURL` blob-url |
| N7 | `url-dialog.svelte:22-23` | `VALID_EXTS` | 导入 `IMAGE_EXTS`/`VIDEO_EXTS` | 重新定义了常量列表，存在漂移风险 |
| N8 | `config.ts:131` | `_cleanPublicDir` | `cleanPublicDir` | TypeScript 中不需要下划线前缀，`private` 关键字已足够 |
| N9 | `topbar-menu.ts:237` | 返回类型 | `MenuItem[]` | 返回类型为 `any[]`；失去 IDE 自动补全和类型安全 |
| N10 | `bgRender.ts` | 扁平函数导出 | 无变更 / 可考虑类 | 函数名清晰（`changeOpacity`、`changeBlur`），但由于共享模块级状态，无法静态分析。可能适合用类重构 |

### 注释覆盖率
大多数文件没有函数级 JSDoc。例外：
- `setting-utils.ts` — 有部分文档注释
- `path.ts` — 有中文块注释解释规范
- `settings/settings.svelte` 这类 Svelte 组件 — Svelte 社区通常依赖清晰的模板语法，所以尚可接受

对于希望社区贡献的插件，建议至少为公共导出项添加一句话摘要。

---

## 3. 性能瓶颈

| # | 严重度 | 位置 | 问题 | 影响 |
|---|--------|------|------|------|
| P1 | ⚠️ 中 | `sourceManager.ts:21-44` | **`scanAll` 串行扫描** — 每个资产和本地目录通过 `for...of` + `await` 串行处理。5 个目录 = 5 次串行网络/FS 调用。 | 对 2-3 个目录可忽略；对 10 个以上目录来说总耗时等于各耗时之和。改用 `Promise.all` 并行化。 |
| P2 | ⚠️ 中 | `sources-tab.svelte:40-93` | **`refreshAll` 串行扫描** — 与 P1 相同。每个分组在同一个 `for...of` 循环体中等待前一个完成。 | 与 P1 相同 |
| P3 | ⚠️ 中 | `asset-picker.svelte:51-69` | **挂载时串行 `readDirItems` / `scanDir`** — 第二个循环（`for...of`）中每个根条目都会调用 `scanDir` 并等待完成。 | `Promise.all` 并行化`scanDir` 调用 |
| P4 | 💡 低 | `topbar-menu.ts:62-85` | **`pickMultipleFiles` 串行上传** — 每个文件在 `for` 循环中单独上传并等待。 | 对小于 10 个文件可忽略；N 个文件＝N 次串行 HTTP POST。可用受控并发池（例如同时 5 个）改进。 |
| P5 | 💡 低 | `sources-tab.svelte:205-217` | **`loadPreview` 无防抖** — 鼠标在文件上快速移动时会为每个 hover 事件触发 `fetch()` + `blob()`。已有正确的 `revokeObjectURL` 清理。 | 添加入口侧 150ms 防抖效果更好。 |
| P6 | 💡 低 | `sourceManager.ts:90-102` | **`pickRandom` 会创建一个新的过滤数组** — `items.filter()` 对每个排除请求分配 O(n) 内存。 | 在仅有排除计数时才使用重试循环（无 `Array.filter`），仅在重试耗尽时才回退过滤。 |
| P7 | 💡 低 | `configStore.setAndSave` | **缺少批量合并** — 短时间内多次调用（例如 `randomSelect` 调用 `setAndSave("currentFile", …)`，紧接着调用 `applyBackground` → `changeOpacity` → `setAndSave`…），每一次都会立即保存。 | 低影响；后台的 localStorage/kernel 调用很轻量。如果速度是关注点，可以用 `batchSave` 模式。 |
| P8 | ✅ 好 | `stores/config.ts:60-68` | **`save()` 中的脏标志守卫** — `if (!this.dirty || !this.ready) return`。是个好的模式。 | 无需操作。 |
| P9 | ✅ 好 | `config-tab.svelte` | **拖拽滑块时用 `oninput` 实时预览，用 `onchange` 持久化** — 避免拖拽时高频 API 调用。 | 无需操作。 |

### 不存在的问题
- 无 N+1 查询模式（一次性读取目录，逐个处理文件）
- 无同步阻塞（全部 async/await）
- 无锁/互斥问题（单线程运行时）

---

## 总结

**优点**：模块边界清晰，依赖方向总体良好，`oninput`/`onchange` 分离很智能，无效配置迁移逻辑完善。

**待修复的前 3 项**：

1. 🔴 提取 `topbar-menu.ts` 和 `sources-tab.svelte` 之间重复的上传/对话框逻辑
2. 🔴 修复 `config-tab.svelte:22` 中仅调用 `renderImage()` 而忽略视频类型的 bug
3. ⚠️ 修复 `utils/fs.ts → stores/config.ts` 的依赖反转；将 `isLocalPath` 移到它应该在的地方

**可快速优化的点**：将 `scanAll`/`refreshAll` 中的 `for...of` + `await` 循环改为 `Promise.all`，以并行化 I/O。

## 问题回复

### 1. I3 UI 重复代码提取到 `services/sourceManager.ts`？

**不太合适。** `sourceManager.ts` 是纯数据服务层（扫描、过滤、随机选取），不应知道 DOM/文件选择器/对话框。那些重复的函数（`pickMultipleFiles`, `pickFolderFiles`, `showXxxDialog`）本质是 **UI 动作工厂** — 创建 `<input>` 元素、调用 `svelteDialog`。放在 service 层会违反依赖方向。

**建议**：提取到 `ui/dialogs/` 作为共享 UI 模块，供 `topbar-menu.ts` 和 `sources-tab.svelte` 共同引用。

### 2. Dialog 组件放到 `ui/dialogs/`？

**合理。** 当前这些散落在 `ui/` 根：

```
ui/
├── local-dir-dialog.svelte    # → ui/dialogs/
├── url-dialog.svelte          # → ui/dialogs/
├── sources/asset-picker.svelte # → ui/dialogs/ (或保留)
```

加上共享的上传/选择动作工厂函数，`ui/dialogs/` 成为独立子模块，职责清晰。

### 3. `libs/setting-utils.ts` vs `utils/settings.ts`？

保持 `libs/` 不变。按现有规则：

| 目录 | 职责 |
|------|------|
| `libs/` | 框架级封装，无本插件业务依赖 |
| `utils/` | 依赖本插件业务上下文 |

`setting-utils.ts` 只依赖 `siyuan` 的 `Plugin`/`Setting`，零业务依赖，应当留在 `libs/`。

命名上 `setting-utils.ts` 的 "utils" 和 `utils/` 目录重叠，容易混淆。建议改为：

- `libs/siyuan-setting.ts` — 明确表达是思源 Setting 的封装
- 或 `libs/setting.ts` — 简洁，类名 `SettingUtils` 已经体现了 "utils" 语义

## 综合架构优化方案

### 目标结构

```
src/
├── index.ts                          # 入口（缩减 ~180 行）
├── types.ts                          # 纯类型定义
├── constants.ts                      # + classifyFileType, - diyIcon 重命名
│
├── libs/                             # 框架级
│   ├── index.d.ts
│   ├── siyuan-setting.ts            # 重命名自 setting-utils.ts
│   └── dialog.ts                     # svelteDialog / confirmDialog
│
├── stores/
│   └── config.ts                     # + isLocalPath, 重命名 post → siyuanApiPost
│
├── services/
│   ├── bgRender.ts                   # 修复 config-tab 调用的视频分派
│   └── sourceManager.ts             # Promise.all 并行化, 重命名 readDirKernel
│
├── utils/
│   ├── api.ts                        # + siyuanApiPost, readDir → readSiyuanDir
│   ├── fs.ts                         # - isLocalPath (移入 stores), - 与 configStore 解耦
│   ├── logger.ts                     # log → devLog, debug → devDebug
│   ├── path.ts                       # 不变
│   └── theme.ts                      # 不变
│
└── ui/
    ├── topbar-menu.ts                # 剥离上传逻辑，引用 ui/dialogs/
    ├── settings/
    │   ├── settings.svelte
    │   ├── config-tab.svelte          # 修复视频 bug, render→dispatch
    │   ├── sources-tab.svelte         # 剥离上传逻辑, refreshAll 并行化
    │   ├── theme-tab.svelte
    │   ├── advanced-tab.svelte
    │   └── about-tab.svelte
    ├── dialogs/                       # 🆕 新目录
    │   ├── index.ts                   # showLocalDir, showUrl, showAssetsDir, pickFiles, pickFolder
    │   ├── local-dir-dialog.svelte
    │   ├── url-dialog.svelte
    │   └── asset-picker.svelte        # 从 sources/ 移入，并行化 onMount
    └── sources/
        └── source-list.svelte         # （仍作为独立组件引用）
```

### 具体变更清单

| # | 类别 | 变更 | 涉及文件 |
|---|------|------|---------|
| A1 | 解耦 | `isLocalPath()` 从 `utils/fs.ts` 移入 `stores/config.ts`，接受 `localFolders` 数组参数，不依赖 store 实例 | `utils/fs.ts`, `stores/config.ts` |
| A2 | 分离 | `classifyFileType()` 从 `types.ts` 移入 `constants.ts`（它只依赖 `IMAGE_EXTS`/`VIDEO_EXTS`） | `types.ts`, `constants.ts` |
| A3 | 提取 | `pickMultipleFiles`, `pickFolderFiles`, `showLocalDirDialog`, `showUrlDialog`, `showAssetsDirDialog` → `ui/dialogs/index.ts` 作为纯函数导出 | `topbar-menu.ts`, `sources-tab.svelte`, `ui/dialogs/index.ts` |
| A4 | 移动 | `local-dir-dialog.svelte`, `url-dialog.svelte`, `sources/asset-picker.svelte` → `ui/dialogs/` | 3 个 svelte 文件 |
| A5 | 修复 | `config-tab.svelte:handleActivateChange` 改用 `bgRender.render(currentFile)` 统一分派 | `config-tab.svelte` |
| A6 | 统一 | `topbar-menu.ts` 的 `pickMultipleFiles` 改用 `utils/api.ts` 的 `putFile`（不再用原始 `fetchPost`） | `topbar-menu.ts` |
| A7 | 并行 | `sourceManager.scanAll` / `sources-tab.refreshAll` / `asset-picker.onMount` 的 `for...of` 改为 `Promise.all` | `sourceManager.ts`, `sources-tab.svelte`, `asset-picker.svelte` |
| A8 | 并行 | `pickMultipleFiles`/`pickFolderFiles` 上传循环用受控并发（`Promise.all` + `map`） | `ui/dialogs/index.ts` |
| A9 | 去重 | `validatePath` 中内联 `require('fs/promises')` 改用 `utils/fs.ts` 的 `getFsp`/`fileExistsLocal` | `sourceManager.ts` |
| A10 | 去重 | `url-dialog.svelte` 中 `VALID_EXTS` 移除，导入 `constants.ts` 的 `IMAGE_EXTS`/`VIDEO_EXTS` | `url-dialog.svelte` |
| A11 | 重命名 | 见下表 | 多个文件 |

#### 重命名表

| 当前 | 新名称 | 位置 |
|------|--------|------|
| `post()` | `siyuanApiPost()` | `utils/api.ts` |
| `readDir()` | `readSiyuanDir()` | `utils/api.ts` |
| `log()` | `devLog()` | `utils/logger.ts` |
| `debug()` | `devDebug()` | `utils/logger.ts` |
| `diyIcon` | `pluginTopIcon` | `constants.ts` |
| `prevUrl` | `previewObjectUrl` | `sources-tab.svelte` |
| `_cleanPublicDir()` | `cleanPublicDir()` | `stores/config.ts` |
| `buildAddBackgroundSubmenu` 返回值 | `MenuItem[]` (显式类型) | `topbar-menu.ts` |
| `setting-utils.ts` | `siyuan-setting.ts` | `libs/` |

### 依赖方向变化（优化后）

```
utils/ 层                            stores/ 层
  fs.ts ──(不再依赖)──→              config.ts (+ isLocalPath)
  api.ts                           
  logger.ts                         
  path.ts                          

services/                           ui/
  sourceManager.ts ─→ utils/{fs,api,path}    topbar-menu.ts ┐
  bgRender.ts      ─→ constants               sources-tab    ├→ ui/dialogs/ (共享)
                                               config-tab    ┘
```

### 不做的事

| 事项 | 理由 |
|------|------|
| `bgRender.ts` 改写为类 | 单例插件场景下模块级状态可接受，重写为类会产生不必要的模板代码，且会破坏所有现有 `import { renderImage } ...` 的调用方式 |
| `loadPreview` 加防抖 | 当前已有 `revokeObjectURL` 清理，fetch 只会对真正显示的预览发起一次请求（`selectPreview` 已做 URL 判等守卫），实际不会重复请求 |
| `pickRandom` 改为重试循环 | 文件数 < 10000 时 `Array.filter` 开销可忽略，代码简洁性优先 |

Good. Now let me also check the test file for sourceManager, and the vitest.setup.ts to understand mock setup.

Let me now execute:

Commit 1 changes:
1. Move `isLocalPath` from `utils/fs.ts` to `stores/config.ts` (as a method or standalone function that takes localFolders parameter)
2. Move `classifyFileType` from `types.ts` to `constants.ts`
3. Rename `diyIcon` to `pluginTopIcon`

Actually, let me reconsider A1. The user said `utils/fs.ts` shouldn't depend on configStore. The function `isLocalPath` calls `configStore.get("localFolders")`. 

Options:
a) Make `isLocalPath` a method on ConfigStore (takes a path, checks against stored localFolders)
b) Make `isLocalPath` accept `localFolders` as a parameter (pure function), then the callers pass in `configStore.get("localFolders")`

Option (b) is cleaner - it keeps the function pure while allowing the callers to decide where localFolders come from. But `isLocalPath` is exported from fs.ts - let me check who calls it.

Let me search.

</details>

```
57:                 return
58:             }
59: 
60:             let lastUrl = ""
61: 
62:             for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
63:                 const file = files[i]
64:                 try {
65:                     const formData = new FormData()
66:                     formData.append("path", `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${file.name}`)
67:                     formData.append("isDir", "false")
68:                     formData.append("modTime", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())
69:                     formData.append("file", file)
70: 
71:                     await new Promise<void>((resolve) => {
72:                         fetchPost("/api/file/putFile", formData, (res: any) => {
73:                             if (res.code === 0) {
74:                                 lastUrl = getFileUrl(
75:                                     `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${file.name}`,
76:                                     'upload'
77:                                 )
78:                             }
79:                             resolve()
80:                         })
81:                     })
82:                 } catch (e) {
83:                     console.warn('[bgCover] upload failed:', file.name, e)
84:                 }
85:             }
86:

88:                 log("[bgCover] menu: pickMultipleFiles done, lastUrl =", lastUrl)
89:                 configStore.set("currentFile", lastUrl)

158:     function pickFolderFiles() {

162:         input.style.display = 'none'

166:             if (!files || files.length === 0) {
167:                 document.body.removeChild(input)
168:                 return
169:             }
170: 
171:             const validFiles: File[] = []
172:             for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
173:                 if (classifyFileType(files[i].name) !== null) {
174:                     validFiles.push(files[i])
175:                 }
176:             }
177: 
178:             if (validFiles.length === 0) {
179:                 document.body.removeChild(input)
180:                 return
181:             }
182: 
183:             if (validFiles.length >= 30) {
184:                 const confirmed = await new Promise<boolean>((resolve) => {
185:                     confirmDialog({
186:                         title: i18n.bulkUploadTitle,
187:                         content: (i18n.bulkUploadWarning).replace('{count}', String(validFiles.length)),                        confirm: () => resolve(true),
188:                         cancel: () => resolve(false),
189:                         width: "420px",
190:                     })
191:                 })
192:                 if (!confirmed) {
193:                     document.body.removeChild(input)
194:                     return
195:                 }
196:             }
197: 
198:             let lastUrl = ""
199: 
200:             for (const file of validFiles) {

202:                     const ok = await apiPutFile(

205:                     )

208:                             `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${file.name}`,

214:                 }
215:             }
```
