**Commit 4: 并行化 I/O**

### A7: Parallelize scanAll in sourceManager.ts
Currently:
```ts
const uploadItems = await scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)
results.push(...uploadItems)

for (const dir of assetDirs) {
    const items = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')
    results.push(...items)
}

if (isDesktop()) {
    for (const dir of localFolders) {
        const items = await scanSource('local', dir)
        results.push(...items)
    }
}
```

Change to: scan upload, all assets, and all locals in parallel using Promise.all.

### A7: Parallelize refreshAll in sources-tab.svelte
Same pattern.

### A7: Parallelize onMount in asset-picker.svelte
Currently:
```ts
for (const item of items) {
    const { imageCount, videoCount, hasSubdirs } = await scanDir(nodePath)
    roots.push(...)
}
```

Change to Promise.all.

### A8: Parallelize uploads
In dialogs/index.ts, the `pickMultipleFiles` and `pickFolderFiles` upload sequentially. Change to concurrent uploads with Promise.all.

For pickMultipleFiles, the files are processed one at a time. We can use Promise.all with map to upload all in parallel:
```ts
const results = await Promise.all(
    Array.from(files).map(file => uploadSingleFileForm(file).catch(() => null))
)
```

But this might overwhelm the backend. A concurrency limit would be better, but for simplicity let's just use Promise.all since the number of files is typically small.

Actually, let me be more conservative. Let me use Promise.all without a concurrency limiter since:
1. Files are typically < 100
2. The backend is local
3. Each file is a small HTTP request

Let me implement.

Actually, thinking about this more carefully: for `pickFolderFiles`, the files are already filtered to valid files and the uploads go through `putFile` which is async. Currently sequential. Change to Promise.all.

For `pickMultipleFiles`, similarly use Promise.all.

Let me also make the scan in `scanAll` parallel. The key insight is that upload, each asset dir, and each local folder are independent.

</details>

  "oldString": "export async function scanAll(\n    assetDirs: string[] = [],\n    localFolders: string[] = [],\n): Promise<ImageItem[]> {\n    const results: ImageItem[] = []\n\n    const uploadItems = await scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)\n    results.push(...uploadItems)\n    debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll upload: ${uploadItems.length} 个文件`)\n\n    for (const dir of assetDirs) {\n        if (dir.length === 0) continue\n        const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)\n        const path = `/data/${normalized}`\n        const items = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')\n        results.push(...items)\n        debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll assets[${dir}]: ${items.length} 个文件`)\n    }\n\n    if (isDesktop()) {\n        for (const dir of localFolders) {\n            if (dir.length === 0) continue\n            const ok = await validatePath(dir)\n            if (!ok) {\n                debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local[${dir}]: 路径不可访问，跳过`)\n                continue\n            }\n            const items = await scanSource('local', dir)\n            results.push(...items)\n            debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local[${dir}]: ${items.length} 个文件`)\n        }\n    } else {\n        debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local: 非桌面端，跳过 ${localFolders.length} 个本地文件夹`)\n    }\n\n    debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll total: ${results.length} 个文件`)\n    return results\n}",
  "newString": "export async function scanAll(\n    assetDirs: string[] = [],\n    localFolders: string[] = [],\n): Promise<ImageItem[]> {\n    const tasks: Promise<ImageItem[]>[] = [\n        scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir),\n    ]\n\n    const validAssetDirs = assetDirs.filter(d => d.length > 0)\n        .map(dir => {\n            const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)\n            return `/data/${normalized}`\n        })\n    tasks.push(...validAssetDirs.map(path => scanSource('assets', path + '/')))\n\n    if (isDesktop()) {\n        const validLocalDirs = localFolders.filter(d => d.length > 0)\n        for (const dir of validLocalDirs) {\n            const ok = await validatePath(dir)\n            if (!ok) {\n                debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local[${dir}]: 路径不可访问，跳过`)\n            } else {\n                tasks.push(scanSource('local', dir))\n            }\n        }\n    } else {\n        debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local: 非桌面端，跳过 ${localFolders.length} 个本地文件夹`)\n    }\n\n    const batch = await Promise.all(tasks)\n    const results = batch.flat()\n    debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll total: ${results.length} 个文件`)\n    return results\n}"
}

  "newString": "    async function refreshAll() {\n        const newGroups: SourceGroup[] = []\n\n        const uploadFiles = await scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)\n        newGroups.push({\n            type: 'upload',\n            label: i18n.pluginCache,\n            path: pluginAssetsDir,\n            removable: false,\n            files: uploadFiles,\n            inaccessible: false,\n            collapsed: false,\n            configKey: '',\n        })\n\n        const assetDirs = configStore.get(\"assetDirs\").filter(Boolean)\n        const localFolders = isDesktop() ? configStore.get(\"localFolders\").filter(Boolean) : []\n\n        const assetTasks = assetDirs.map(async (dir) => {\n            const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)\n            const path = `/data/${normalized}`\n            const label = normalized.startsWith('assets/') ? normalized.slice('assets/'.length) : normalized\n            const files = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')\n            return { type: 'assets' as const, label, path, files, normalized }\n        })\n\n        const localTasks = localFolders.map(async (dir) => {\n            const files = await scanSource('local', dir + (dir.endsWith('/') ? 💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

There are still 2 `post(` calls left in config.ts:
```
const files = await post<any[]>("/api/file/readDir", {
```
and 
```
            const files = await post<any[]>("/api/file/readDir", {
```

These were in the `cleanOldConfigIfNeeded` and `cleanPublicDir` methods. My perl regex `(?<![a-zA-Z])(?<!fetch)post\(` might not have caught them because of the `<any[]>` generic in between. Let me check...

Actually wait, the regex `(?<![a-zA-Z])(?<!fetch)post\(` should match `post<any[]>("` because `post<` has `post` followed by `<`, not `(`. The regex looks for `post(` specifically. But `post<any[]>(` has a generic between `post` and `(`.

Let me just manually fix these 2 remaining occurrences.

</details>

全部完成。5 个 commit，73 个测试全部通过。

## 总结

| Commit | 变更要点 |
|--------|---------|
| `231fa64` | **解耦** `utils/fs.ts` 移除对 `stores/config.ts` 的依赖，`classifyFileType` 移入 `constants.ts`，`diyIcon` → `pluginTopIcon` |
| `3fea8dd` | **提取** `ui/dialogs/` 共享模块 — 消除 `topbar-menu.ts` 与 `sources-tab.svelte` 之间的重复上传/对话框逻辑 (~300 行减少) |
| `ed4782b` | **修复** `config-tab` 视频分派 bug，统一上传 API（不用原始 `fetchPost`），去重 `VALID_EXTS`/`validatePath` |
| `ce4cac1` | **并行化** `scanAll`、`refreshAll`、`asset-picker onMount`、批量上传 — 用 `Promise.all` 替代 `for...of+await` |
| `d4c7c21` | **重命名** 8 项：`post`→`siyuanApiPost`、`readDir`→`readSiyuanDir`、`log`→`devLog`、`debug`→`devDebug`、`prevUrl`→`previewObjectUrl`、`_cleanPublicDir`→`cleanPublicDir`、`setting-utils.ts`→`siyuan-setting.ts`、`buildAddBackgroundSubmenu` 返回类型 |

最终结构图：

```
src/
├── libs/
│   ├── siyuan-setting.ts         ← 重命名
│   └── dialog.ts
├── stores/
│   └── config.ts                 ← + isLocalPath, + siyuanApiPost
├── utils/
│   ├── fs.ts                     ← - isLocalPath, - configStore import
│   ├── api.ts                    ← readSiyuanDir
│   ├── logger.ts                 ← devLog / devDebug
│   └── ...
├── services/                     ← Promise.all 并行化
└── ui/
    ├── dialogs/                  ← 🆕 共享对话框
    │   ├── index.ts
    │   ├── local-dir-dialog.svelte
    │   ├── url-dialog.svelte
    │   └── asset-picker.svelte
    └── settings/
```

Svelte convention: Svelte doesn't enforce any specific file naming convention. The Svelte documentation and most examples use PascalCase for components (`Button.svelte`, `App.svelte`). However, in practice:
- Component files are often PascalCase
- Non-component files follow whatever convention the project uses

两件事：先澄清规范现状，再评估统一命名的合理性。

## Svelte 文件名规范

**Svelte 不强制任何命名规范。** 官方文档和社区示例中，组件文件通常用 PascalCase（`Button.svelte`、`App.svelte`），因为组件名在模板中用作标签时需要 PascalCase。但这只是约定，Svelte 编译器不关心文件名。

## 当前项目命名现状

实际存在三种风格混用：

| 风格 | 文件 | 
|------|------|
| **camelCase** | `services/bgRender.ts`, `services/sourceManager.ts` |
| **kebab-case** | 所有 `.svelte` 文件 + `libs/siyuan-setting.ts` + `ui/topbar-menu.ts` |
| **lowercase** | `config.ts`, `api.ts`, `fs.ts`, `logger.ts`, `path.ts`, `theme.ts`, `dialog.ts`, `index.ts`, `types.ts`, `constants.ts` |

不一致的根本原因是：
- `.ts` 文件大多沿袭原始纯 TS 项目（pre-Vite/Svelte 迁移）的 lowercase 风格
- 新增的 `services/` 用了 camelCase（你的 repo）
- `.svelte` 文件用了 kebab-case（Svelte 5 示例项目 `plugin-sample-vite-svelte` 的惯例）

## 统一方案对比

| 方案 | Svelte 组件 | .ts 模块 | 优点 | 缺点 |
|------|-----------|----------|------|------|
| **A: 全 PascalCase** | `ConfigTab.svelte` | `BgRender.ts` | Svelte 官方推荐风格 | .ts 文件 PascalCase 非社区惯例 |
| **B: 全 camelCase** | `configTab.svelte` | `bgRender.ts` | 与 `services/` 现有一致，JS/TS 社区惯例 | Svelte 社区不太常见 |
| **C: Svelte=PascalCase, ts=camelCase** | `ConfigTab.svelte` | `bgRender.ts` | 各自社区最佳实践 | svelte 与 .ts 文件名格式不统一 |
| **D: 保持 kebab-case** | `config-tab.svelte` | `bg-render.ts` | URL-friendly，思源 `plugin-sample-vite-svelte` 惯用 | services/ 需要改名 |

## 建议

**方案 D**（全项目 kebab-case）与你的参考项目 `plugin-sample-vite-svelte` 一致，且：
- 你的 Svelte 文件、`siyuan-setting.ts`、`topbar-menu.ts` 已经用 kebab-case
- 只需改 `services/bgRender.ts` → `services/bg-render.ts` 和 `services/sourceManager.ts` → `services/source-manager.ts`（加更新所有 import）
- lowercase 文件（`api.ts`, `fs.ts` 等）无需改，因为已经是单词级别的 kebab-case 子集

需要我按方案 D 出具体变更清单吗？にゃ～♡

   Actually wait, with Vite you need to specify the filename. `Index.svelte` with capital I. Let me check...

   With Vite, `import X from "./ui/settings"` will look for `./ui/settings/index.svelte` or `./ui/settings.svelte`. If the file is `Index.svelte` (capital I), Vite might not resolve it from `./ui/settings/` because it looks for `index` (lowercase). This depends on the Vite/Svelte plugin configuration. 

   Actually, most Vite setups with `resolve.mainFields` and Svelte plugin DO resolve `./dir/` to `./dir/index.svelte` (lowercase). `Index.svelte` with capital I might NOT work with directory resolution.

   So the choice is:
   - `index.svelte` (lowercase) — works with Vite directory resolution, but breaks PascalCase convention
   - `Settings.svelte` — follows PascalCase, keeps explicit path `./settings/Settings.svelte`

   I think `Settings.svelte` is the safer and more consistent choice. Using `index.svelte` with lowercase 'i' goes against the PascalCase convention. Let me recommend `Settings.svelte`.

   - Consistent with PascalCase convention for Svelte files
   - No ambiguity with Vite resolution
   - Avoids the lowercase 'i' exception to PascalCase

## 方案 C：Svelte = PascalCase / .ts = camelCase

### `settings.svelte` vs `index.svelte`

**推荐 `Settings.svelte`**。理由：

- Vite 目录解析 (`import X from "./settings"`) 查找的是 `index.svelte`（**小写 i**），而小写 `index` 会破坏 PascalCase 约定，造成特例
- `Index.svelte`（大写 I）在 Linux 下**不会**被 Vite 自动解析为目录入口
- `Settings.svelte` 保持 PascalCase 一致，路径显式：`"../settings/Settings.svelte"`，无歧义

Ah, the PascalCase files are untracked! The `git add -A` didn't pick them up because... hmm, `-A` should add all files including untracked. Maybe there was an issue with the `&&` chain in my commit command.

Actually, looking at my commit command:
```
git add -A && git diff --cached --stat -- src/ tests/ 2>/dev/null; git reset HEAD ".agents/" 2>/dev/null; git reset HEAD "tests/ui/sources/" 2>/dev/null; git commit -m "..."
```

The `git reset HEAD "tests/ui/sources/"` might have happened after `git add -A` but before `git commit`. The `&&` and `;` operators... let me trace:
1. `git add -A` - succeeds, stages everything
2. `git diff --cached --stat -- src/ tests/ 2>/dev/null` - succeeds, shows stat
3. `git reset HEAD ".agents/"` - unstages agents files, succeeds
4. `git reset HEAD "tests/ui/sources/"` - This was supposed to be a separate reset. But actually this might have been a mistake - it unstaged the source-list test which I wanted deleted.

Wait, I used `;` between some commands and `&&` between others. Let me re-read:
```
git add -A && git diff --cached --stat -- src/ tests/ 2>/dev/null; git reset HEAD ".agents/" 2>/dev/null; git reset HEAD "tests/ui/sources/" 2>/dev/null; git commit -m "..."
```

The `&&` chains `add -A` to `diff`. The `;` then runs `git reset` regardless of whether the previous command succeeded. And then `;` runs the next `git reset`. And then `;` runs `git commit`.

But `git reset HEAD "tests/ui/sources/"` would unstage the test file deletion... but the test file was under `tests/`, not `src/`. So the `git diff` with `-- src/ tests/` showed the staged changes, but then `git reset HEAD "tests/ui/sources/"` unstaged it from the commit.

The main problem: the PascalCase svelte files are UNTRACKED. This means `git add -A` didn't add them. Why?

Oh wait - `git add -A` should add untracked files. Let me just add them now and amend the commit.

Actually, let me just add them in a new commit (Commit 2 for the .ts renames) alongside the .ts renames.

</details>

4:

6: |------|------|------|

28:

30: |------|------|
31: | 源文件 | `public/i18n/<lang>.json`，扁平 JSON 键值对 |
32: | 构建 | Vite 自动将 `public/` 内容输出到 `dist/`（`i18n/` 子目录） |
33: | 运行时 | 思源自动读 `i18n/` 目录注入 `this.i18n`，无需手动加载 |
34: | 代码中使用 | `this.i18n.keyName` 直接访问，支持 `${var}` 模板插值 |
35: | 命令快捷键显示 | `addCommand({ langKey: "selectManual", hotkey: "⇧⌘F6" })` |
36: | plugin.json | `displayName` / `description` / `readme` 字段支持 `{ "default": "...", "zh_CN": "..." }` |

<path>/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/.agents/rules/api-fs-rules.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: # 思源 API 与本地文件系统调用规则
2: 
3: ## 三种源类型的核心差异
4: 
5: | 源类型 | 平台 | 目录枚举 | Canvas 渲染 URL |
6: |--------|------|---------|-----------------|
7: | `local` | **desktop only** | `require('fs/promises')`（`src/utils/fs.ts`） | `url("file:///absolute/path/img.jpg")` |
8: | `upload` | 全平台 | 思源 API `readDir` | `url("public/{packageName}/img.jpg")` |
9: | `assets` | 全平台 | 思源 API `readDir` | `url("assets/.../img.jpg")` |
10: 
11: ---
12: 
13: ## 一、源码模块职责
14: 
15: ### `src/utils/fs.ts` — 本地文件系统（仅 `local` 源类型）
16: 
17: ```
18: isDesktop()           → typeof window.require === 'function' && getFsp() !== null
19: readLocalDir(path)    → fsp.readdir + isFile() 过滤，仅返回 name[]
20: getFileUrl(path, type)→ 按 sourceType 构造渲染 URL
21: fileExists(path)      → fsp.access 检测
22: ```
23: 
24: **原则**：仅用于 `localFolders` 配置项。禁止操作 `data/...` 工作空间路径。
25: 
26: ### `src/utils/api.ts` — 思源内核 API（`upload` / `assets` 源类型）
27: 
28: ```
29: readDir(path)    → /api/file/readDir   → 自动过滤 isDir，返回 name[]
30: putFile(path, blob) → /api/file/putFile → FormData + 原始 Blob
31: removeFile(path) → /api/file/removeFile
32: downloadUrl(url) → fetch + putFile 一站式
33: ```
34: 
35: **原则**：全平台可用，统一用 `fetchSyncPost`（Promise-based）。
36: 
37: ---
38: 
39: ## 二、Canvas 渲染 URL 构造
40: 
41: canvas CSS 中引用背景图片时，URL 按源类型不同：
42: 
43: | sourceType | Canvas `url()` | 说明 |
44: |-----------|---------------|------|
45: | `local` | `url("file:///home/user/Pictures/img.jpg")` | 绝对路径，仅 desktop 可用 |
46: | `upload` | `url("public/{packageName}/img.jpg")` | 思源 webview 相对路径，全平台 |
47: | `assets` | `url("assets/.../img.jpg")` | 思源 webview 相对路径，全平台 |
48: 
49: > **`file:///` 仅用于 `local`**。`upload` 和 `assets` 在所有平台（含 desktop）都使用思源 webview 的相对路径，思源内核负责解析到正确位置。
50: 
51: ### upload 路径: `data/` → `public/` 前缀转换
52: 
53: upload 文件存在 `/data/public/{plugin}/` 下，但 canvas CSS 中引用时去掉 `data` 前缀：
54: 
55: ```typescript
56: let rel = apiPath
57: if (rel.startsWith('/data/')) rel = rel.slice(1)        // /data/public/... → data/public/...
58: if (rel.startsWith('data/')) rel = '/' + rel.slice(5)    // data/public/...  → /public/...
59: // 最终用于 canvas: url("public/{plugin}/img.jpg")
60: ```
61: 
62: ---
63: 
64: ## 三、目录枚举 dispatch
65: 
66: ```typescript
67: // sourceManager.scanSource 中
68: const filenames = type === 'local'
69:     ? await readLocalDir(path)       // fsp.readdir
70:     : await readDirKernel(path)      // fetchSyncPost → /api/file/readDir
71: ```
72: 
73: ### 判断路径是否属于 localFolders
74: 
75: ```typescript
76: // ✅ 正确：查 localFolders 配置
77: function isLocalPath(path: string): boolean {
78:     return configStore.get("localFolders").some(f => path.startsWith(f))
79: }
80: 
81: // ❌ 错误：前缀匹配不可靠
82: path.startsWith('/')     // /data/public/... 也以 / 开头
83: path.startsWith('data/') // localFolders 可能是 /home/user/...
84: ```
85: 
86: ---
87: 
88: ## 四、`/api/file/putFile` 上传规范
89: 
90: ### 必须使用 FormData + 原始 File/Blob
91: 
92: ```typescript
93: const fd = new FormData()
94: fd.append("path", "data/public/{plugin}/file.jpg")
95: fd.append("isDir", "false")
96: fd.append("modTime", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())
97: fd.append("file", rawFile)  // 原始 File 或 Blob
98: fetchSyncPost("/api/file/putFile", fd)
99: ```
100: 
101: > `putFile` 是 HTTP Multipart form 接口，后端从 `FormData.file` 读取二进制流。JSON body 会导致 `ERR_CONNECTION_RESET`。
102: 
103: ---
104: 
105: ## 五、禁止事项
106: 
107: | 禁止 | 原因 |
108: |------|------|
109: | 对 `data/...` 路径调用 `fsp.readdir` | 相对路径 → ENOENT |
110: | 用 `startsWith('/')` 判断本地路径 | `/data/public/...` 也以 `/` 开头 |
111: | `putFile` 用 JSON body | 后端只接受 FormData |
112: | `fs.ts` 中 import `api.ts` 的函数 | 职责分离 |

(End of file - total 112 lines)
</content>
```

38: 
39: 粘贴操作不触发 `keydown`。

42: <script>
43:     let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
44: 
45:     function handleInput() {
46:         if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
47:         debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(url.trim()), 500)
48:     }
49: </script>
50: 
51: <input bind:value={url} oninput={handleInput} />
52: <!-- Enter 仅用于确认，非检测 -->
53: ```

60: 
61: `webkitdirectory` 在 Electron 不同版本下 `files[0].path` 行为不一致（有时只返回文件夹名）。改用自定义 Dialog：
62: 
63: ```

65: │  添加本地目录                         │
66: ├──────────────────────────────────────┤
67: │  路径: [___________________________] │  文本输入（oninput 防抖 500ms）
68: ├──────────────────────────────────────┤
69: │  发现 48 张图片, 3 个视频 — ✅        │  fsp.access → fsp.readdir → classifyFileType
70: ├──────────────────────────────────────┤
71: │                              [添加]  │
72: └──────────────────────────────────────┘
73: ```
74: 
75: ### 多文件选择：`<input multiple accept="image/*,video/*">`
76: 
77: ```typescript
78: const input = document.createElement('input')
79: input.type = 'file'
80: input.multiple = true
81: input.accept = 'image/*,video/*'
82: input.onchange = () => { /* process files */ }
83: input.click()
84: ```
85: 
86: ### 整个目录选择：`<input webkitdirectory>`
87: 
88: ```typescript

90: input.type = 'file'
91: input.setAttribute('webkitdirectory', '')
92: input.onchange = async () => {
93:     const validFiles = [...files].filter(f => classifyFileType(f.name) !== null)
94:     // ≥ 30 文件时需 confirmDialog 确认
95: }
96: input.click()
97: ```

<content>
1: ## 实现思路
2: 
3: 在 `<HTML>`中元素中添加一个和 `<head>` 与 `<body>` 平级的`<canvas>`元素和`<video>`元素，平铺居中且处于笔记最底层，用来存放图片背景。随后通过给 `<body>` 整体添加 `style='opacity: xxx'` 属性来实现笔记面板的透明。不要修改 `<canvas>`元素和`<video>`元素的透明度。
4: 
5: 用户可设置的透明度定义域为 `[0.1, 1]`。但为了笔记内容的可读性，使用加权逻辑 `f(x) = 0.99 - 0.25x`，加权后透明度值域为 `[0.74, 0.99]`。由于不同主题本身就有完全不同的颜色设定，所以同样的透明度设置在不同的主题上表现不完全一致。
6: 
7: ## 背景资源文件管理
8: 
9: 用户可以选择：
10: 
11: - 仅桌面端激活
12:     - 链接本地目录，选择本地文件夹，读取其中的图片和视频文件作为背景资源
13: 
14: - 所有平台：
15:     - 链接资源目录（思源笔记数据目录/data/assets中的文件夹）
16:     - 上传多个文件（"upload" -> ）
17:     - 上传整个目录 ("upload")，上传本地文件夹中所有图片，
18:     - 添加网络资源 ("url"), 下载网络图片到资源目录。

**Title:** .agents/rules/api-fs-rules.md

```json
{
  "filePath": "/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/.agents/rules/api-fs-rules.md",
  "oldString": "## 四、`/api/file/putFile` 上传规范\n\n### 必须使用 FormData + 原始 File/Blob\n\n```typescript\nconst fd = new FormData()\nfd.append(\"path\", \"data/public/{plugin}/file.jpg\")\nfd.append(\"isDir\", \"false\")\nfd.append(\"modTime\", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())\nfd.append(\"file\", rawFile)  // 原始 File 或 Blob\nfetchSyncPost(\"/api/file/putFile\", fd)\n```\n\n> `putFile` 是 HTTP Multipart form 接口，后端从 `FormData.file` 读取二进制流。JSON body 会导致 `ERR_CONNECTION_RESET`。\n\n---\n\n## 五、禁止事项\n\n| 禁止 | 原因 |\n|------|------|\n| 对 `data/...` 路径调用 `fsp.readdir` | 相对路径 → ENOENT |\n| 用 `startsWith('/')` 判断本地路径 | `/data/public/...` 也以 `/` 开头 |\n| `putFile` 用 JSON body | 后端只接受 FormData |\n| `fs.ts` 中 import `api.ts` 的函数 | 职责分离 |",
  "newString": "## 四、`/api/file/putFile` 上传规范\n\n### 必须使用 FormData + 原始 File/Blob\n\n```typescript\nconst fd = new FormData()\nfd.append(\"path\", \"data/public/{plugin}/file.jpg\")\nfd.append(\"isDir\", \"false\")\nfd.append(\"modTime\", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())\nfd.append(\"file\", rawFile)  // 原始 File 或 Blob\nfetchSyncPost(\"/api/file/putFile\", fd)\n```\n\n> `putFile` 是 HTTP Multipart form 接口，后端从 `FormData.file` 读取二进制流。JSON body 会导致 `ERR_CONNECTION_RESET`。\n\n### 统一使用 `utils/api.ts` 的 `putFile()` 封装\n\n所有上传操作（含 `topbarMenu`、`sources-tab`、`dialogs`）必须通过 `utils/api.ts` 的 `putFile()` 函数，禁止在各处直接用 `fetchPost` 构造 FormData：\n\n```typescript\n// ✅ 正确：通过 api.ts 封装\nimport { putFile } from \"../utils/api\"\nawait putFile(`data/public/plugin/${file.name}`, file)\n\n// ❌ 错误：各处重复构造 FormData + raw fetchPost\nconst fd = new FormData()\nfd.append(\"path\", ...)\nfetchPost(\"/api/file/putFile\", fd, callback)\n```\n\n### 批量上传并行化\n\n```typescript\n// ✅ 正确：Promise.all 并行上传\nconst results = await Promise.all(\n    files.map(f =>\n        putFile(`data/public/plugin/${f.name}`, f).catch(() => false)\n    )\n)\n\n// ❌ 错误：串行 for 循环\nfor (const file of files) {\n    await putFile(`data/public/plugin/${file.name}`, file)\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 五、禁止事项\n\n| 禁止 | 原因 |\n|------|------|\n| 对 `data/...` 路径调用 `fsp.readdir` | 相对路径 → ENOENT |\n| 用 `startsWith('/')` 判断本地路径 | `/data/public/...` 也以 `/` 开头 |\n| `putFile` 用 JSON body | 后端只接受 FormData |\n| `fs.ts` 中 import `api.ts` 的函数 | 职责分离 |\n| `fs.ts` 中 import `stores/config.ts` | 低层工具不应依赖状态层 |\n| 各处重复构造 FormData + raw fetchPost | 必须统一用 `api.ts` 的 `putFile()` |\n| `for...of` + `await` 串行扫描/上传 | 用 `Promise.all` 并行化 |\n| 在 `url-dialog` 中硬编码 `VALID_EXTS` | 用 `IMAGE_EXTS.union(VIDEO_EXTS)` 从 constants 导入 |"
}
```

Edit applied successfully.
